| `YearToQuarterEndConsolidatedStatementOfComprehensiveIncomeSingleStatementTextBlock` | `string` | 四半期連結累計期間 |
| `YearToQuarterEndConsolidatedStatementOfComprehensiveIncomeSingleStatementUSGAAPTextBlock` | `string` | 四半期連結累計期間 |
| `YearToQuarterEndConsolidatedStatementOfComprehensiveIncomeTextBlock` | `string` | 四半期連結累計期間 |
| `YearToQuarterEndConsolidatedStatementOfComprehensiveIncomeUSGAAPTextBlock` | `string` | 四半期連結累計期間 |
